}

  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]

  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)

    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;

    score := s;

  }

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert Sum(t[..|t|-1]) == Sum(s[..i]);
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(t[..|t|-1]) + t[|t|-1];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
  assert Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1) * m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) == Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert Sum(a[..k]) <= (k-1) * m + m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)

    i := i + 1;

    score := m;
  }

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert Sum(t[..|t|-1]) == Sum(s[..i]);  // use the definition of Sum
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(t[..|t|-1]) + t[|t|-1];
  assert t[|t|-1] == s[i];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert Sum(a[..k-1]) >= 0;
    assert Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1) * m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) == Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert Sum(a[..k]) >= Sum(a[..k-1]) >= 0;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) <= (k-1) * m + a[k-1] <= (k-1) * m + m == k * m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert t[|t|-1] == s[i];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1] <= (k-1)*m + m;
    assert (k-1)*m + m == k*m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k*m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  // The following two lines are tautologies that make the proof
  // of the lemma succeed without changing the program semantics.
  assert s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]];
  assert Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    // Base case: Sum of zero elements is 0, which is in the required range.
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..0]) <= 0 * m;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    // From the invariant of the recursive call and the bounds on a[k-1]
    // we can deduce the required bound for Sum(a[..k]).
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k - 1) * m;
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) == Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= (k - 1) * m + m;
    assert (k - 1) * m + m == k * m;
  }
}

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }

  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  // We need to establish both conclusions explicitly.
  // First, the slice equality:
  assert s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]];
  // Second, the sum equality:
  assert Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
    assert 0 <= 0 <= 0 * m;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;

    // Adding a[k-1] gives the desired bounds for k.
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];

    // Simplify the right-hand side:
    assert (k-1) * m + m == k * m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m;
  }
}

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert Sum(t[..|t|-1]) == Sum(s[..i]);          // from the induction hypothesis
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(t[..|t|-1]) + t[|t|-1];    // by definition of Sum
  assert t[|t|-1] == s[i];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
    assert 0 <= 0 <= 0 * m;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) == Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1) * m;
    assert Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1] <= (k-1) * m + m;
    assert (k-1) * m + m == k * m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert Sum(t[..|t|-1]) == Sum(s[..i]) by {
    // By definition of Sum, Sum(t[..|t|-1]) == Sum(s[..i])
    // because t[..|t|-1] = s[..i]
    assert Sum(t[..|t|-1]) == Sum(s[..i]) by {
      // t[..|t|-1] == s[..i] so the sums are equal
    }
  }
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(t[..|t|-1]) + t[|t|-1] by {
    // Sum of a sequence equals sum of its prefix plus last element
    assert Sum(t) == Sum(t[..|t|-1]) + t[|t|-1] by {
      // By definition of Sum over a sequence
    }
  }
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0 by {
      // Sum of empty sequence is 0
    }
    assert 0 <= 0 <= 0 * m;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) == Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert Sum(a[..k-1]) >= 0 by {
      // From induction hypothesis: 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1])
    }
    assert Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1) * m by {
      // From induction hypothesis
    }
    assert Sum(a[..k]) <= (k-1) * m + a[k-1] <= (k-1) * m + m == k * m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) >= 0;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    // Use SumAppend to prove that appending a[i] works
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {

{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1) * m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert t[|t|-1] == s[i];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(t[..|t|-1]) + t[|t|-1];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1) * m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= (k-1) * m + m;
    assert (k-1) * m + m == k * m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

  decreases |a|

// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be

  requires |a| > 0

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert Sum(t[..|t|-1]) == Sum(s[..i]);  // use the induction on Sum
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(t[..|t|-1]) + t[|t|-1];
  assert t[|t|-1] == s[i];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)

  decreases k

    assert (k-1) * m + m == k * m;

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert t[|t|-1] == s[i];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(t[..|t|-1]) + t[|t|-1];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
  assert t == s[..i] + [s[i]];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
    assert 0 <= 0 <= 0 * m;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) == Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1) * m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) <= (k-1) * m + a[k-1];
    assert Sum(a[..k]) <= (k-1) * m + m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k]);
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert t[|t|-1] == s[i];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(t[..|t|-1]) + t[|t|-1];
  assert Sum(t[..|t|-1]) == Sum(s[..i]);
  assert t[|t|-1] == s[i];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
    assert 0 <= 0 <= 0 * m;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) == Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1) * m;
    assert a[k-1] <= m;
    assert Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1] <= (k-1) * m + m == k * m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
  assert Achievable(a, m, score);
}

  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]

  assert Sum(t) == Sum(t[..|t|-1]) + t[|t|-1];

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert Sum(t[..|t|-1]) == Sum(s[..i]); // sum of the prefix
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(t[..|t|-1]) + t[|t|-1];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
  assert s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
    assert 0 <= 0 <= 0 * m;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) == Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1) * m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1] <= (k-1) * m + m;
    assert (k-1) * m + m == k * m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
  // Postcondition Achievable
  assert 0 <= score <= m;
  assert Sum(a) - score >= 0;
  assert Sum(a) - score <= (|a| - 1) * m;
  // Postcondition maximality
  assert forall v | score < v <= m :: !(0 <= v <= m && Sum(a) - v >= 0 && Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m);
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  // By definition of Sum for a tail of length zero
  assert Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    // Sum of an empty prefix is 0.
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    // By the ValidScores predicate, the current element is bounded.
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  // From the definition of Sum, we can deduce the second postcondition
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(t[..|t|-1]) + t[|t|-1];
  assert Sum(t[..|t|-1]) == Sum(s[..i]); // because t[..|t|-1] == s[..i]
  assert t[|t|-1] == s[i]; // because t == s[..i+1]
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i] ==> Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];

--- LLM RESPONSE (807 tokens, 9.07s) ---
<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert t[|t|-1] == s[i];
  assert Sum(t[..|t|-1]) == Sum(s[..i]); // uses SumAppend recursively
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(t[..|t|-1]) + t[|t|-1];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) == Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1) * m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) <= (k-1) * m + a[k-1];
    assert Sum(a[..k]) <= (k-1) * m + m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    assert 0 <= i < |a|;
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

--- LLM RESPONSE (815 tokens, 8.88s) ---
<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert t[|t|-1] == s[i];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(t[..|t|-1]) + t[|t|-1];
  assert Sum(t[..|t|-1]) == Sum(s[..i]); // from earlier lemma
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
    assert 0 <= 0 <= 0 * m;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) == Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1) * m;
    assert Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1] <= (k-1) * m + m;
    assert (k-1) * m + m == k * m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

  decreases |a|

}

{

}

  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(t[..|t|-1]) + t[|t|-1];
  assert Sum(t[..|t|-1]) == Sum(s[..i]);
  assert t[|t|-1] == s[i];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) == Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1) * m;
    assert Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1] <= (k-1) * m + m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)

  var i := 0;

    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].

  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert t[|t|-1] == s[i];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(t[..|t|-1]) + t[|t|-1];
  assert Sum(t[..|t|-1]) == Sum(s[..i]);
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1) * m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1] <= (k-1) * m + m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert Sum(t[..|t|-1]) == Sum(s[..i]); // Sum of prefix
  // t[..|t|-1] is s[..i], and t[|t|-1] is s[i]
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(t[..|t|-1]) + t[|t|-1];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    // using inductive hypothesis: 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1)*m
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1) * m;
    // add a[k-1] to both bounds
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1] <= (k-1)*m + m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}
